id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><h2><strong style="color: #6f6f6e; font-size: 8pt;"><font style="color: #000000;"><em style="font-size: small;">Smith &amp; Wesson</em></font></strong></h2> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong><font style="color: #000000;"><em style="font-size: small;"> <span>M&amp;P Shield 9mm 3.1 Inch Barrel Black Melonite Finish Polymer Frame One 7 Round and One 8 Round Magazine</span></em></font></strong></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span>Extremely thin and lightweight design means that it can be comfortably carried all day. Single-sided thumb safety and slide stop maximize slimness. M&amp;P s patented take down lever and sear deactivation system allows for disassembly without pulling the trigger. Includes 2 magazines; 1 with extended capacity for full grip. 18 degree grip angle for natural point of aim. Striker-fired for short and consistent trigger pull every time. White dot front sight, white 2 dot rear sight. Stainless steel barrel and slide with polymer frame. Black Melonite 68 HRc barrel/slide finish.</span></font></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><font size="2">Available in 9mm and .40 S&amp;W, the new M&amp;P SHIELD features a slim design combined with the proven and trusted features found in the M&amp;P Pistol Series. From the pistols easily concealed one-inch profile to its optimized 18-degree grip angle, the M&amp;P SHIELD offers professional-grade features that provide consumers with simple operation and reliable performance. </font></p> <p><font size="2">Chambered in 9mm and .40 S&amp;W for proven stopping power, the M&amp;P SHIELD features a high-strength polymer frame with a black, Melonite coated stainless steel slide and barrel. Both models are standard with a 3.1-inch barrel, which contributes to an overall length of 6.1 inches and an unloaded weight of 19 ounces. For fast tracking and smooth target acquisition, the M&amp;P SHIELD is standard with a 5.3-inch sight radius and has been enhanced with a short, consistent trigger pull measuring 6.5 pounds. Featuring a quick and audible reset made possible by the striker-fired action, the M&amp;P SHIELD allows multiple rounds to be placed on target both consistently and accurately. </font></p> <p><font size="2">ALL BACKED BY THE SMITH &amp; WESSON LIFETIME SERVICE POLICY.</font></p> <p class="p1">Officially unveiled at the 2012 NRA Show, the new M&amp;P SHIELD is a powerful, slim, lightweight, and concealable polymer pistol. Produced in our state-of-the-art manufacturing facility in Springfield, Massachusetts, at standards designed to deliver the utmost in quality and dependability, the M&amp;P SHIELD delivers outstanding consistency in comfort, accuracy and performance in a carry or concealed carry platform.</p> <table class="t1" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="624"> <tbody> <tr> <td class="td1" valign="middle"> <p class="p1"><span class="s1"><strong>The M&amp;P SHIELD</strong></span>was designed as an extension of our highly successful M&amp;P pistol line, a platform which Armorers are very familiar with. Comfort and confidence are the first impressions felt when handling the new M&amp;P SHIELD but it delivers high marks on performance as well by incorporating many of the following proven, professional grade features found in our full size M&amp;P pistol.</p> </td> </tr> <tr> <td class="td1" valign="middle"> <table class="t1" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="624"> <tbody> <tr> <td class="td2" valign="middle"> <p class="p2">&nbsp;</p> </td> <td class="td3" valign="middle"> <p class="p1"> Striker fired action providing a smooth, short, consistent and dependable trigger pull</p> <p class="p1"> Stainless steel internal chassis reducing flex and providing a stable shooting platform&nbsp;</p> <p class="p1"> Patented take down lever and sear deactivation system allowing service without pulling the trigger&nbsp;</p> <p class="p1"> Optimized 18 degree grip angle providing a natural point of aim and rapid target acquisition</p> <p class="p1">&nbsp;</p> </td> </tr> <tr> <td class="td4" colspan="2" valign="middle"> <p class="p3"><span class="s1"><strong>The M&amp;P SHIELD</strong></span>is chambered in both 9mm and .40 S&amp;W[<span class="s2"><strong>1</strong></span>] and, comes standard with two magazines one compact for easy concealment and the other extended for full grip and increased capacity - both are features not offered by our competition! With an MSRP of $449 and the backing of Smith &amp; Wessons lifetime service policy, we believe the M&amp;P SHIELD is destined to become the standard for professional grade concealed carry.</p> </td> </tr> </tbody> </table> </td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p class="p1">&nbsp;</p> <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"> <tbody> <tr> <td class="td1" valign="middle"> <p class="p1"><span class="s1"><strong>1 </strong></span>California and Massachusetts compliant models are currently in development and we anticipate availability within CY12</p> </td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <p class="p1">&nbsp;</p> <p><font size="2"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/SW/sw_shield_c.jpg" alt="" width="544" height="251"><br></font></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul id="attributeListTableId" class="specs"> <li class="first clearfix"><span class="name">SKU:</span><span class="value">180021<br></span></li> <li class="clearfix"><span class="name">Model:</span><span class="value">M&amp;P9 SHIELD<br></span></li> <li class="clearfix"><span class="name">Caliber:</span><span class="value">9mm<br></span></li> <li class="clearfix"><span class="name">Capacity:</span><span class="value">7 Round &amp; I got an early version. However, I found it too big for my pocket and sold it for a Kahr CM9. A few months later, I missed it and bought another. I then got a Sig P938 and sold the Shield. Last week I bought my third Shield. I was looking for a single stack gun that I could fit all of my fingers on. I can just about do it with my Sig but the Sig is small. The Shield fits my hand very well with the extended grip and is a little larger than my Sig. It will be used as my belt gun. There is something about the Shield that keeps drawing me to it.
